				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
						NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						has_opinion = { target = ROOT value > -25 }
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = political_outreach }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }

	#EU Policies
	focus = {
		id = SLV_EU001
		icon = align_to_europe
		
		x = 13
		y = 10
		#relative_position_id = #has to be ajusted
		
		cost = 5
		prerequisite = {
		}
		#mutually_exclusive = { }
		available = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = tooltip_focus_EU001_availability
			hidden_trigger = {
				#additional  availability
			} #End of hidden_trigger
			} #End of custom_trigger_tooltip
		}
		historical_ai = {
		}
		#select_effect = { }
		bypass = {
		}
		cancel = { }
		cancel_if_invalid = no
		continue_if_invalid = yes
		available_if_capitulated = no
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_focus_EU001
			hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = -0.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}

				add = 40
				date > 2000.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}

					OR = {

					else_if = {

						original_tag = ENG

					}
			}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU206
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
						modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than

					}

					}

				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						OR = {

							original_tag = ENG
						}
					}

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2000.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}

				add = -10

							var = eurosceptic

					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2016.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10

						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }
					}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = EUU
					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = eurosceptic
						value = 0.25
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }

			}

					}

							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic < 0 }

						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
					has_global_flag = european_constitution
					has_global_flag = treaty_of_lisbon
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU402
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2019.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}

				add = 40

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10

						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic

							compare = greater_than

					}

					}
				}
					add_to_variable = {

						value = 0.3
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { eurosceptic > 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { eurosceptic = 1 }

				set_country_flag = focus_EU601_QMV
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = focus_EU601
			}
			} #hidden_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				date > 2004.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				all_country = {
					OR = {
							AND = {
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
								any_of = {
									array = influence_array
									value = v
									index = i
									if = {
										limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
										set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
										always = yes
									}
									else = { always = no }
								}
								check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
								check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.05 }
							}
							tag = PREV
							NOT = { has_idea = EU_member }
					}
				}
			}
			### Euroscepticism
			modifier = {
				add = 20
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.4
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -40
					ROOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than
						}
					}
			}
		}
	}
